 iske tahat google drive main watsap ke chats byaap difolt taur par diya jayega

 haalanki yah gambhir samasya nahin he, kyonki agar aap hameshaa byaap lete hai yaa phir chats aapke smartphone main hai to wo delit nahin honge
 Under the partnership with Google, keeping backups of whatsapp chats on Google Drive will not reduce the space given to you
 google drive parwotsapachats byaap rakhane kaa phayda ye he ki ise kisi bhi smartphone par aasaani se open kar sakate hai
 If you have taken a new phone or are using a new smartphone for whatsapp, then this feature will prove beneficial for you
 google drive par watsap kaa byaap lene ke liye apane smartphone google drive ko actevet kar len
 To make a backup, go to the main menu of whatsapp and tap on Settings
 yahaan chat kaa opshan hoga yahaan aap byaap tu google drive select kar sakate hai
 Here you will get the option of backup frequency which you can choose according to your choice

 Users of the company are advised to connect the phone to wifi while backing up, as backup files differ in size and consume data, which can cost you extra data
 gauratlab he kiwotsapacat byaap system duusare chating ap se alag he
 Because whatsapp's chats and media are stored on the phone instead of being stored in a detached service

 The country's highest civilian honor Bharat Ratna was instituted in 1954
 tab se ab tak 41 logon ko isse nawaja ja chukaa he, lekin inamen se koi bhi khilaadi nahin he
 Actually, the reason is a rule attached to it
 niyamon ke mutabik bharat ratna kala, sahitya or vigyaan ke vikaas main asaadhaaran seva ke liye tathaa sarvocch str kii jan seva ke liye diya jaataa he
 There is no mention of sports in it
 jabaki padam puraskaron ke niyamon ke tahat yah puraskaar sabhi prakaar ke kshetron jaise ki kala, sahitya, shiksha, khel-kud, chikitsa, saamaajik kaary, vigyaan, ejiniyari, saarvajanik maamle, civil seva, vyapaar or udyog aadi main vishisht or asaadhaaran uplabdhiyon yaa sevaaon ke liye die jate hai

 Till about a decade ago, the youth used to express love to someone through love letters
 nae daur ke miseging ap ne ab lav letters ko jaise hameshaa ke liye ateet kii deevaaron main chunavaa diya ho
 It was the magic of 'pyaar Bhari Paati' that filmmakers put songs on the same theme in many films
 kai filmon ke tital isi par rakhe gaye
 Sequences of repeated love letter writing, tearing up, and passing it on to Dilruba and Jaanman were filmed in many films
 par ab yah kareeb-kareeb har taraf se nadaarad he
 The reality is also seen in films
 ab to mobile par beep-beep kii aawaaj ke jariye hi badi aasaani se 'ai lav you' ke massej bheje jate hai, whatsapp, vibar, hike jaise miseging ap ise or khushnuma ehsaas karaane ko taiyaar milte hai
 The new methods of ezhar-e-ishq are certainly convenient, but the old love letter used to be different
 kabhi letters ke bheetar gulab kii pankhudiyaan, kabhi rajnigandha kaa spray, kabhi pink color se dil kii akruti
 
 
 The means and ways of expressing love with each phase may have changed, but this love is immortal
 'likhe jo khat tuje', 'maine khat mehboob ke naam likhaa', 'pyaar ke kaagaj pe, dil kii kalam se' jaise geet aaj bhi yuva dilon kii dhadakanen badhaate hai

 The Supreme Court on Wednesday reserved its verdict on the plea of pakistani terrorist Ajmal Amir Kasab, convicted and sentenced to death in the 2008 Mumbai terror attack
 kasaab ne faansee kii sajaa barkaraar rakhane vaale bombay ucch nyaayalay ke faisle ko chunauti di he The death sentence of Kasab was upheld by the Bombay High Court on 21 February 2011
 mumbai kii ek nichali adaalat ne chah may 2010 ko kasaab ko faansee kii sajaa sunai
 Among other charges, Kasab has also been convicted of waging war against the country
 nyaayamurti aftab alam evam nyaayamurti sike prasad kii khandpeeth ne teen maheenon se adhik samay tak chali bahason ke nishkarsh par apana faisla surakshit rakh liya
 Hearing on Kasab's plea in the court started from 31 January last
 faansee kii sajaa ko chunauti dene vaali kasaab kii yachika par sunwaayee puri karne ke baad nyaayalay ab sah-aaropee fahim harshad mohammad yusuf ansaari evam sabauddin shaikh ko chode jane ko chunauti dene vaali maharashtra sarkaar kii yachika par sunwaayee karegaa
 Kasab argued that he did not have a fair trial as he was not provided legal assistance which is mandatory in terms of Article 22 (1) of the Indian Constitution

 2- experiment se dare nahin:dhoni ek aise captain rahe hai, jo kabhi bhi experiment karne se peeche nahin hate

 The International Maritime Law Tribunal (tribunal) also referred to the case as falling under its jurisdiction
 tribunel ke jaj ne kaha, 'italy or bharat donon sabhi adalati sunwaayiyon ko nilambit karenge or aisi nai sunwaayee shuru karne se parhez karenge jisase vivaad badhata ho yaa koi nirnay dene ke liye khatra athwa purvaagrah paidaa ho

 â€™ Diwali Health Tips In Hindi: Diwali is on 27th October
 is hindu tyohaar ko duniyabar main manaaya jaataa he
 This festival, celebrated for 5 days, begins with Dhanteras and ends with Narak Chaturthi or Chhoti Diwali, Govardhan Pooja and then Bhai Dooj (bhai Dooj)
 lekin diwali ke maukey par asthma (asthma) se peedit hai
 Diwali evening and few days after that can be very difficult for people suffering from respiratory problems
 isaki do vajahen hai ek to diwali (diwali) par hone vaala pradooshan or doosraa badalata mausam
